***ontkleden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontkleden.html>ontkleden</a> (56444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-, dis-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleden.html>kleden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dress</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontkleden.html>ontkleden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To undress, disrobe someone or something</li>
<li><i>The reflexive form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontkleden.html>ontkleden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used</i> as an intransitive form: To undress oneself, get naked</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To 'dismantle' something by removing a cover</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To (lay) bare, disclose, unveil, reveal</li>
<li><i>The reflexive form <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontkleden.html>ontkleden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> ...</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used</i> as an intransitive form: To rid oneself, dispose (of ...)</li></ol>

***ontkrachten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontkrachten.html>ontkrachten</a> (44942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kracht.html>kracht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontkrachten.html>ontkrachten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to diminish the force or strength of, to take the edge off</li>
<li>to refute</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontlasten.html>ontlasten</a> (24832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">last</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">load</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontlasten.html>ontlasten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unburden, to relieve (a load)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to relieve (from a duty)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to relieve oneself, to move one's bowel</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontlenen.html>ontlenen</a> (73875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lenen.html>lenen</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontlenen.html>ontlenen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to borrow, to derive
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woord.html>woord</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:alfabet.html>alfabet</a>' <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontlenen.html>ontleend</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> alpha (Œ±) <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> beta (Œ≤), <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Griekse <a href = vnd.unilang:alfabet.html>alfabet</a>.</i> ‚Äî The word 'alphabet' <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>derived</b> from alpha (Œ±) and beta (Œ≤), the first two <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> of the Greek alphabet.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontmoeten.html>ontmoeten</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">untmuten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">entmuten</i>, corresponding to <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a></i>. The latter verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*muoten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*m≈çtijanƒÖ</i>.
</p><p>The unprefixed form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cognate Low German <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">m√∂ten</i>, West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">moetsje</i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">meet</i>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">m√∏de</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to meet</li>
<li>to encounter, come across</li></ol>
